} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd7a200d19547dc4a6ef60b70870fb24de5eca26b') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '9e8167c09371bdb0c49165a2176bb98f633a67b2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd7a200d19547dc4a6ef60b70870fb24de5eca26b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus_base.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') != '0ad4319bebb3baa29efde83975998dc6c516addc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '0ad4319bebb3baa29efde83975998dc6c516addc') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '678687a917e1b5499c7ddf6179cdfe663e69d7c2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.css') !== '0ad4319bebb3baa29efde83975998dc6c516addc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'bf08db0f32b46cf2da1e2affc73639c3ade3dc86') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'bf08db0f32b46cf2da1e2affc73639c3ade3dc86') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'fcbdc0013fc679070cad1a904a1b072d789c67d8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'bf08db0f32b46cf2da1e2affc73639c3ade3dc86') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
